                function mouseMove()
                {
                    try
                    {
                       var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                       var event = window.event || arguments.callee.caller.arguments[0];


                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                         {
                              if
                              (
                               event.layerX > 940 |
                               event.layerX <= 0 |
                               event.layerY <= 0
                               )
                               {
                                   return;
                               }

                         }
                         else
                         {
                              if
                              (
                               event.offsetX > 940 |
                               event.offsetX <= 0 |
                               event.offsetY <= 0
                               )
                               {
                                   return;
                               }
                           }

                        var divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                      var divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                        var divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
//                      if(divMoveHor == null | divMoveVer == null)
                        if(divMoveHor == null)
                        {
                            createDiv();
                            divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                          divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                            divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
                        }

                        divMoveHor.style.left = event.clientX - 53;
                        divMoveHor.style.top = 0;
//                      divMoveVer.style.left = 0;
//                      divMoveVer.style.top = event.clientY - 29;

                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.layerY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.layerX;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.offsetY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.offsetX;
                        }

                        if(currentPositionX < 250)//鼠标与上边框的距离不足div的高度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX + 50;//div出现在鼠标下方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX - 250;;//否则，div出现在鼠标上方

                        }
                        if(currnetPositionY < 150)//鼠标与左边框的距离不足div的宽度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY + 50;//div出现在鼠标右方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY-150;
                        }

                        var aa;
                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.layerX];
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.offsetX];
                        }

                        var str_table = "";
                        if(Is_Apple() == true||ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox"){
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color: rgba(255,192,203,0.3);\">";
                        }
                        else{
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color:pink;filter:alpha(opacity=30,Style=0)\">";
                        }




                        divDetailVer.innerHTML = str_table
//                                                +"<tr>"
//                                                +"<td style=\"font-size:12px;font-weight:bold\">"
//                                                +"日期：<br>"
//                                                +"</td>"
//                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"日期"
                                                + mDateTime
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell0+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"开盘价"
                                                +mOpenPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell1+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"收盘价"
                                                +mClosePrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell2+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"最高价"
                                                +mHighestPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell3+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"最低价"
                                                +mLowestPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell4+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"</table>";
                    }
                    catch(e)
                    {}
                }
                function createDiv()
                {
                    //纵向线
                    //xiewei var moveDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveHor' style='background-color:#666666; width:1px;  height:551px;'></div>");
                    var moveDiv = document.createElement("div");
                    moveDiv.setAttribute("id","divMoveHor");
                    moveDiv.style.cssText = "background-color:#666666; width:1px;  height:551px;";

                    moveDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    moveDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    moveDiv.style.top = ge('divid').style.top;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv);

                    //横向线
//                    var moveDiv1 = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveVer' style='background-color:#666666; height:1px; width:977px;overflow:hidden;'> </div>");
//                    moveDiv1.style.position ='absolute';
//                    moveDiv1.style.visibility='visible';
//                    moveDiv1.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
//                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv1);

                    //提示框
                    //xiewei var detailDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divDetailVer' style='width:120px; height:32px;'></div>");
                    var detailDiv = document.createElement("divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.setAttribute("id","divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.style.cssText = "width:140px; height:32px;";

                    detailDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    detailDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    detailDiv.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(detailDiv);
                }
        </script>

                function mouseMove()
                {
                    try
                    {
                       var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                       var event = window.event || arguments.callee.caller.arguments[0];


                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                         {
                              if
                              (
                               event.layerX > 940 |
                               event.layerX <= 0 |
                               event.layerY <= 0
                               )
                               {
                                   return;
                               }

                         }
                         else
                         {
                              if
                              (
                               event.offsetX > 940 |
                               event.offsetX <= 0 |
                               event.offsetY <= 0
                               )
                               {
                                   return;
                               }
                           }

                        var divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                      var divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                        var divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
//                      if(divMoveHor == null | divMoveVer == null)
                        if(divMoveHor == null)
                        {
                            createDiv();
                            divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                          divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                            divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
                        }

                        divMoveHor.style.left = event.clientX - 53;
                        divMoveHor.style.top = 0;
//                      divMoveVer.style.left = 0;
//                      divMoveVer.style.top = event.clientY - 29;

                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.layerY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.layerX;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.offsetY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.offsetX;
                        }

                        if(currentPositionX < 250)//鼠标与上边框的距离不足div的高度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX + 50;//div出现在鼠标下方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX - 250;;//否则，div出现在鼠标上方

                        }
                        if(currnetPositionY < 150)//鼠标与左边框的距离不足div的宽度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY + 50;//div出现在鼠标右方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY-150;
                        }

                        var aa;
                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.layerX];
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.offsetX];
                        }

                        var str_table = "";
                        if(Is_Apple() == true||ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox"){
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color: rgba(255,192,203,0.3);\">";
                        }
                        else{
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color:pink;filter:alpha(opacity=30,Style=0)\">";
                        }




                        divDetailVer.innerHTML = str_table
//                                                +"<tr>"
//                                                +"<td style=\"font-size:12px;font-weight:bold\">"
//                                                +"日期：<br>"
//                                                +"</td>"
//                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"日期"
                                                + mDateTime
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell0+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"开盘价"
                                                +mOpenPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell1+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"收盘价"
                                                +mClosePrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell2+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"最高价"
                                                +mHighestPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell3+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"最低价"
                                                +mLowestPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell4+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"</table>";
                    }
                    catch(e)
                    {}
                }
                function createDiv()
                {
                    //纵向线
                    //xiewei var moveDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveHor' style='background-color:#666666; width:1px;  height:551px;'></div>");
                    var moveDiv = document.createElement("div");
                    moveDiv.setAttribute("id","divMoveHor");
                    moveDiv.style.cssText = "background-color:#666666; width:1px;  height:551px;";

                    moveDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    moveDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    moveDiv.style.top = ge('divid').style.top;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv);

                    //横向线
//                    var moveDiv1 = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveVer' style='background-color:#666666; height:1px; width:977px;overflow:hidden;'> </div>");
//                    moveDiv1.style.position ='absolute';
//                    moveDiv1.style.visibility='visible';
//                    moveDiv1.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
//                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv1);

                    //提示框
                    //xiewei var detailDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divDetailVer' style='width:120px; height:32px;'></div>");
                    var detailDiv = document.createElement("divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.setAttribute("id","divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.style.cssText = "width:140px; height:32px;";

                    detailDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    detailDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    detailDiv.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(detailDiv);
                }
        </script>

                function mouseMove()
                {
                    try
                    {
                       var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                       var event = window.event || arguments.callee.caller.arguments[0];


                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                         {
                              if
                              (
                               event.layerX > 676 |
                               event.layerX <= 0 |
                               event.layerY <= 0
                               )
                               {
                                   return;
                               }

                         }
                         else
                         {
                              if
                              (
                               event.offsetX > 676 |
                               event.offsetX <= 0 |
                               event.offsetY <= 0
                               )
                               {
                                   return;
                               }
                           }

                        var divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                      var divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                        var divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
//                      if(divMoveHor == null | divMoveVer == null)
                        if(divMoveHor == null)
                        {
                            createDiv();
                            divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                          divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                            divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
                        }

                        divMoveHor.style.left = event.clientX - 53;
                        divMoveHor.style.top = 0;
//                      divMoveVer.style.left = 0;
//                      divMoveVer.style.top = event.clientY - 29;

                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.layerY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.layerX;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.offsetY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.offsetX;
                        }

                        if(currentPositionX < 250)//鼠标与上边框的距离不足div的高度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX + 50;//div出现在鼠标下方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX - 250;;//否则，div出现在鼠标上方

                        }
                        if(currnetPositionY < 150)//鼠标与左边框的距离不足div的宽度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY + 50;//div出现在鼠标右方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY-150;
                        }

                        var aa;
                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.layerX];
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.offsetX];
                        }

                        var str_table = "";
                        if(Is_Apple() == true||ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox"){
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color: rgba(255,192,203,0.3);\">";
                        }
                        else{
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color:pink;filter:alpha(opacity=30,Style=0)\">";
                        }




                        divDetailVer.innerHTML = str_table
//                                                +"<tr>"
//                                                +"<td style=\"font-size:12px;font-weight:bold\">"
//                                                +"日期：<br>"
//                                                +"</td>"
//                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"日期"
                                                + mDateTime
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell0+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"开盘价"
                                                +mOpenPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell1+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"收盘价"
                                                +mClosePrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell2+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"最高价"
                                                +mHighestPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell3+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"最低价"
                                                +mLowestPrice
                                                +"："
                                                +aa.cell4+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"</table>";
                    }
                    catch(e)
                    {}
                }
                function createDiv()
                {
                    //纵向线
                    //xiewei var moveDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveHor' style='background-color:#666666; width:1px;  height:551px;'></div>");
                    var moveDiv = document.createElement("div");
                    moveDiv.setAttribute("id","divMoveHor");
                    moveDiv.style.cssText = "background-color:#666666; width:1px;  height:551px;";

                    moveDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    moveDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    moveDiv.style.top = ge('divid').style.top;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv);

                    //横向线
//                    var moveDiv1 = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveVer' style='background-color:#666666; height:1px; width:977px;overflow:hidden;'> </div>");
//                    moveDiv1.style.position ='absolute';
//                    moveDiv1.style.visibility='visible';
//                    moveDiv1.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
//                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv1);

                    //提示框
                    //xiewei var detailDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divDetailVer' style='width:120px; height:32px;'></div>");
                    var detailDiv = document.createElement("divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.setAttribute("id","divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.style.cssText = "width:140px; height:32px;";

                    detailDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    detailDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    detailDiv.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(detailDiv);
                }
        </script>

                function mouseMove()
                {
                    try
                    {
                         var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                         var event = window.event || arguments.callee.caller.arguments[0];
                         if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                         {
                             if
                             (
                              (event.layerX == 0&&event.clientX!=58)|//用event.client!=58是控制只显示曲线图起始点，offsetX为0的坐标值
                               event.layerX > 334 |
                               event.layerX < 0 |
                               event.layerX < 0 |
                               event.layerY <= 0
                               )
                              {
                                  return;
                              }
                         }
                          else
                         {
                             if
                             (
                              (event.offsetX == 0&&event.clientX!=58)|//用event.client!=58是控制只显示曲线图起始点，offsetX为0的坐标值
                               event.offsetX > 334 |
                               event.offsetX < 0 |
                               event.offsetX < 0 |
                               event.offsetY <= 0
                              )
                             {
                                 return;
                             }
                          }
//                        ge('cell0').innerText = dataObjs[event.offsetX].cell0;
//                        ge('cell1').innerText = dataObjs[event.offsetX].cell1;
//                        ge('cell2').innerText = dataObjs[event.offsetX].cell2;

                        var divMoveHor = ge('divMoveHor');
//                      var divMoveVer = ge('divMoveVer');
                        var divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
//                      if(divMoveHor == null | divMoveVer == null)
                        if(divMoveHor == null)
                        {
                            createDiv();
                            divMoveHor =ge('divMoveHor');
//                          divMoveVer =ge('divMoveVer');
                            divDetailVer = ge('divDetailVer');
                        }

                        divMoveHor.style.left = event.clientX  - 58;
                        divMoveHor.style.top = 0;

                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.layerY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.layerX;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                        currentPositionX = event.offsetY;//offsetY鼠标在当前div中的坐标，clientY鼠标在整个屏幕中的坐标
                        currnetPositionY = event.offsetX;
                        }

                        if(currentPositionX < 200)//鼠标与上边框的距离不足div的高度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX + 50;//div出现在鼠标下方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.top = currentPositionX - 200;//否则，div出现在鼠标上方

                        }
                        if(currnetPositionY < 210)//鼠标与左边框的距离不足div的宽度

                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY + 50;//div出现在鼠标右方
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            divDetailVer.style.left = currnetPositionY-210;
                        }

                        var aa;
                        if (ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.layerX];
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            aa = dataObjs[event.offsetX];
                        }
                        var str_table = "";
                        if(Is_Apple() == true||ua.match(/Firefox/i)=="firefox")
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color: rgba(255,192,203,0.3);\">";
                        else
                            str_table = "<table style=\"background-color:pink;filter:alpha(opacity=30,Style=0)\">";

//                      divDetailVer.innerHTML = "<table bgcolor=\"black\" style=\"display:\" style=\"background-color:pink;filter:alpha(opacity=30,Style=0)\">"
                        divDetailVer.innerHTML = str_table
//                                                +"<tr>"
//                                                +"<td style=\"font-size:13px\">"
//                                                +"日期时间：<br>"
//                                                +"</td>"
//                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"日期时间"
                                                +mCurrentDate
                                                +"："+aa.cell0+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"当前价格"
                                                +mCurrentPrice
                                                +"："+aa.cell1+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"<tr>"
                                                +"<td style=\"position:relative;color:black;font-size:13px\">"
                                                //+"涨幅"
                                                +mCurrentRose
                                                +"："+aa.cell2+"<br>"
                                                +"</td>"
                                                +"</tr>"
                                                +"</table>";
                    }
                    catch(e)
                    {}
                }
                function createDiv()
                {
                    try
                    {
                    //纵向线
                    //xiewei var moveDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveHor' style='background-color:#666666; width:1px; height:524px;'></div>");
                    var moveDiv = document.createElement("div");
                    moveDiv.setAttribute("id","divMoveHor");
                    moveDiv.style.cssText = "background-color:#666666; width:1px; height:524px;";

                    moveDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    moveDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    moveDiv.style.top = ge('divid').style.top;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv);
                    //横向线
//                    var moveDiv1 = document.createElement("<div id='divMoveVer' style='background-color:#666666; height:1px; width:889px;overflow:hidden;'> </div>");
//                    moveDiv1.style.position ='absolute';
//                    moveDiv1.style.visibility='visible';
//                    moveDiv1.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
//                    ge('divid').appendChild(moveDiv1);

                    //提示框
                    //xiewei var detailDiv = document.createElement("<div id='divDetailVer' style='width:175px;height:32px;' ></div>");
                    var detailDiv = document.createElement("div");
                    detailDiv.setAttribute("id","divDetailVer");
                    detailDiv.style.cssText = "width:200px;height:32px;";

                    detailDiv.style.position ='absolute';
                    detailDiv.style.visibility='visible';
                    detailDiv.style.left = ge('divid').style.left;
                    ge('divid').appendChild(detailDiv);
                    }
                    catch(e)
                    {

                    }
                }

        </script>
